# SOLAR ENERGY CLAIMS - RANKED BY DATE

**Analysis Summary:**
- Total Claims Extracted: 1893
- Positive Claims: 929
- Negative Claims: 901
- Neutral/Mixed Claims: 63
- Date Range: 2008-02-05 to 2025-12-12
- Source: 561 articles from The Breakthrough Institute

---

Ranked chronologically from oldest to newest.
